 Get started in impressing them today
 
 
 1
 If you are sitting in the office like someone and there is no response from them, do not panic
 jab kabhi vah meeting main hon, kahin or vyast hon, to un ke kaamon main unki madad karen
 Then see how she slowly makes you her hero
 2
 If your girlfriend likes pet, make that pet as well as your choice
 iskaa matlab yah katai na nikaalen ki aap ko apni garlfriend ke kute ko ghumaane le janaa hoga yaa use morning vaak karwaani hogi
 Whenever you go to his house, take some biscuits for the dogs
 unke liye itnaa hi kaaphi he, aap ko pasand karne ke liye
 3
 samay-samay par unhen mail karte rahen
 It is not necessary that you mail or message them when there is any work or on any occasion
 roj ek imail or subah shaam messej bhejne kii aadat daalen
 Despite this, she can give you the fillings that you will not be able to live without getting excited
 4
 Along with helping in the work of the office, sometimes if you do something for your girlfriend, she will give you lots of love
 yah mat sochie ki aapako khaanaa bananaa nahin aata yaa aap us ke liye aisa kya banaaenge, jis se vah khush ho jaaegi
 Just make whatever seems easy, if you want, make Maggi or Popcorn
 yakeenan yah rasta sidhe un ke dil tak ja pahonchega
 5
 roj akhbaar padhein yaa news dekhen, taaki aapako aasapaas ke vishyon kii jaankaree rahe
 Keep an eye on national or foreign news rather than local newspaper
 is kaa phayda yah hoga ki jab kabhi aap ke samaane anchaahi yaa anjaane dibet ke halaat honge, to bhi aap apana aatmavishvaas khoe bagaiyr, apane saathi yaa garlfriend ko impress kar sakenge
 6
 sori jaise shabdon ko mahaj bolen nahin
 Make your partner feel that you are really regretting your mistake
 england ke khilaaf 9 november se shuru hone vaali test siries ke liye bhartiya team kaa elaan kar diya gaya he
 KL Rahul, Shikhar Dhawan and Rohit Sharma have not been able to make it to the team due to injury, while Bhuvneshwar Kumar has also not emerged from the injury
 gautam gambhir kii team main jagah barkaraar he or eshanth sharma kii team main vaapasi hui he
 Gambhir, who returned after a long time in international cricket from the Test series against New Zealand, scored a half-century in the last Test match in Indore
 team main hardik pandya,karun nair or jayant yadav ko shaamil kiya gaya he
 This team has been selected for the first two Tests
 test siries kaa puraa kaarykramengland ke khilaaf rajkot main 9-13 november ke bich hone vaale test se siries kaa aagaaj hoga or bhartiya team 5 november se rajkot main abhyaas shuru karegi
 This is followed by the second in Visakhapatnam between November 17-12, the third in Mohali between November 26-30, the fourth in Mumbai between December 8-12 and the fifth and final Test in Chennai between December 16-20
 england se pichhali teenon test siries haara he bharataisisi test team ranking main sheersh par maujuud bhartiya team ke liye yah shrinkhalaa kisi pariksha ke samaan hogi, kyonki england ke khilaaf pichhali teen test shrinkhalaaon main bharat ko haar mili he

 match ke shuru main sabakuch thik-thaak chal rahaa tha

 boron se tha

 1
 cancer se surakshit rakhata he-kesar main bharpoor maatra main antioxident paae jate hai

 2

 3

 a Facebook user Ayan Saif posted this misleading post on September 25, 2019

 is lekh ke mutabik, yah photo ek syrian bachche kii he jo syria main civil war ke dauraan apni bahan ko bachaane kii koshish kar rahaa he

 a child protecting his sister during a shootout in Syria

 mahoday ab samay aa gaya he ki aap ardh sainikon ko ap kar sakate hai
 They say that BSF, ITBP, SSB are deployed on the 1500 km long border of our country, so why are we not being given paramilitary specials
 jab sena ke jawan ko sarkaar 16,000 foot hit par bhatte ke taur par 21000-31000 rupee de rahi he to itibipi or him veeron ko is tarah kaa bhatta kyon nahin diya ja rahaa he
 The same CISF jawans get 30 days leave in a year while the army and paramilitary forces get 60 days
 is kaaran siaisef ke kai jawan aatmahatya kar lete hai
 Central police forces are not only on the border but also in front of Naxalite affected areas
 aae din is morche par unke javaanon kii maut hoti rahati he

 pension kii bhi maang kar rahe hai

 biguef ke chif ne daawa bhi kiya he ki pakistan ke kai post ko uda diya gaya he
 On June 26, eight CRPF personnel were killed and 20 injured in Pampore, Jammu and Kashmir
 unka kafila srinagar jammu neshnal haive se guzar rahaa tha

 tabhi aatankwaadiyon ne hamalaa kar diya

 haal philhal main sena ke agar chaar jawan shahid hue hai jo biguef ke bhi chaar javaanon ne qurbaani di he

 aatankwaad, ugravad or seemaa par dushmano kaa saamana

 inkaa mukhiya inke kader se nahin hota he

 ipies adhikari banate hai iske chif

 iskaa mukhiya sena kaa adhikari hota he

 - hiranagar sector main paak golabari main gurnam singh shahid (aresapura) - Sushil Kumar Shaheed (kurukshetra) in rspura Sector - aresapura main hi jitendra kumaar shahid (motihaari) Koli Nitin Subhash Shaheed (sangli) in Machil Sector qurbaani ek, shahadat ek magar suvidhaon or inaam main itnaa fark kyon
 This is their complaint
 aatankwaad, ugravad or seemaa par dushmano kaa saamana
 Central Security Forces come under the Union Ministry of Home Affairs
 inkaa mukhiya inke kader se nahin hota he
 The commandants of these security forces do not become the heads of their forces
 ipies adhikari banate hai iske chif
 By the way, in common parlance, we call all forces as paramilitary forces but the paramilitary force is only one, that is Assam Rifles
 iskaa mukhiya sena kaa adhikari hota he
 The rest are Central Armed Police Forces

 to kya shahadat sirf sambodhan main he, adhikaron ke arth main nahin he

 shahadat ke samay kii bhavukta acchhee baat he
 But that sentimentality becomes dramatic when we forget the half-soldiers who fought like soldiers
 guuruuvaar ko haryana ke mukhyamantri manohar laal khatter ne purv sainik ramkishan greval ke parivaar ko das lakh kii madad raashi or ek sadsy ko naukari kaa elaan kiya lekin kaha ki ramkishan ko shahid kahana thik nahin he
 In a way, Khattar saheb is right, but his second point can give relief to the paramilitary force
 khatter sahab ne kaha ki jo seemaa par marataa he vahi shahid he to ardh sainik balon ke jawan kyon shahid nahin maane jate hai
 Former soldier Ramkishan Grewal was cremated in his village
 bhivani zile ke bamala gaanv main unke antim sanskaar main rahul gandhi bhi shariq hue
 Ramkishan had reached the village of Grewal in the morning
 dilli ke mukhyamantri kejariwal bhi vahaan pahunche or ek karod kii raashi dene kaa elaan kiya
 Congress leaders Randeep Surjewala and Dependra Hooda also shoulder the body of Ramkishan Grewal
 jaise shivaraj singh chouhan ne bhopal main ramashankar yadav ko kandhaa diya tha
 In Haryana, Congress does not give party tickets to anyone in the election of sarpanch or panchayat but Union Minister VK Singh said that Ramkishan Grewal had contested sarpanch on Congress ticket
 uski aatmahatya durbhagyapurna he
 His case was about the bank
 van rank van pension kii vajah se nahin tha
 Who gave him a tablet of sulfas
 wo hamaare paas aata or ham help na karte to hamaara kasoor hota
 VK Singh made this statement from Delhi
 unka gaanv ramkishan greval ke gaanv se thodi hi duuri par he
 BJP leader Siddharth Nath Singh said that Rahul Gandhi never did anything about One Rank One Pension
 hamane to isaki kamiyon ko thik karne ke liye cameti bhi banaai he
 BJP MP Satyapal Singh said that he feels that Delhi Police has not handled this issue properly
 purv sainik ke parivaar se milane main kisi ko koi dikkat nahin he
 Shahnawaz Hussain said that so many army soldiers were martyred, Congress leaders and Rahul Gandhi did not go to his funeral
 kisi ne aatmahatya kii he to raajnneeti kar rahe hai
 Shahnawaz's target seems to be a little bit right
 tippaniyan BJP leader Nalin Kohli said that the incident is sad but it has become a photo opportunity for the Congress
 magar congress bijepi kii is aalochana ke baad bhi is maamle ko lekar sakriy nazar aane lagi he
 The Aam Aadmi Party is also very active
 bhivani se laut kar shaam ko rahul gandhi ne jantar mantar par candil march kaa netritv kiya he
 But the police took Rahul Gandhi to his arrest
 do din main rahul gandhi teesri baar ditten kiye gaye hai
 Rahul Gandhi was taken to the Parliament Street police station, later to the Tughlaq Road police station
 tughlaq road par hi unka ghar he
 Spokesperson Manish Tiwari said it was an undisclosed emergency
 tiwari ne kaha ki agar raajnneetik log santvanaa vyakt nahin karenge to or koun karegaa
 By the way, what is the point of detention before candle march at Jantar Mantar
 ek daleel he ki is pradarshan kii ijazat nahin lee gai thi
 Congress says permission was taken

e
 BSF (deployed along Pakistan and Bangladesh border) - bharat tibet seemaa police yani ki itibipi (china se lagi seemaa par tainaat) - Central Industrial Security Force ie CISF - sashastr seemaa bal yani ki esasabi (nepal or bhutan seemaa par) We checked the press release of the Home Ministry from the site of the Press Information Bureau
 15 agast ke din jari ek bayaan main grahamantri rajnath singh ne siarpief ke ek jawan ko shahid kahkar sambodhit kiya he
 So is martyrdom just in address, not in the sense of rights
 aaj aapako twitor or fasebuk par jaakar dekhnaa chahie, ki kitne aise massej hai jo inke haq kii baat karne vaale hai
 The sentimentality of martyrdom is a good thing
 lekin wo bhavukta tab naatakeey ho jaati he jab ham sainikon kii tarah ladane vaale ardh sainikon ko bhul jate hai
 On Thursday, Haryana Chief Minister Manohar Lal Khattar announced a grant of one million rupees to the family of former soldier Ramkishan Grewal and a job to a member but said it was not right to call Ramkishan a martyr
 ek tarah se khatter sahab kii baat thik bhi he lekin unki duusari baat se ardhsainik bal ke jawan ko raahat mil sakati he
 Khattar Saheb said that the one who dies on the border is the martyr, so why are the soldiers of the paramilitary forces not considered martyrs
 purv sainik ramkishan greval kaa antim sanskaar unke gaanv main kiya gaya
 Rahul Gandhi also attended his funeral in Bamla village of Bhiwani district
 subah subah ramkishan greval ke gaanv pahunche the
 Delhi Chief Minister Kejriwal also reached there and announced a sum of one crore
 congress netaa randeep surajevaala or deependra hooda ne ramkishan greval ke shav ko kandhaa bhi diya
 Like when Shivraj Singh Chauhan gave the shoulder to Ramashankar Yadav in Bhopal
 haryana main congress sarpanch yaa panchayat ke chunaav main kisi ko party tikat nahin detii he lekin kendriya mantri ve ke singh ne kaha ki ramkishan greval ne congress ke tikat par sarpanch kaa chunaav ladaa tha
 His suicide is unfortunate
 uskaa maamla bank kaa tha
 One rank was not due to one pension
 use kisne sulphas kii tablet di
 He would have come to us and if we had not helped, we would have been guilty
 ve ke singh ne yah bayaan dilli se diya
 His village is a short distance from the village of Ramkishan Grewal
 bhaajapa netaa siddharth nath singh ne kaha ki rahul gandhi ne van rank van pension ko lekar kabhi kuch nahin kiya
 We have also formed a committee to correct its shortcomings
 bijepi ke saansad satyapal singh ne kaha ki unhen lagata he ki dilli police ne is masale ko thik se handle nahin kiya he
 There is no problem in meeting the family of an ex-soldier
 shahanwaaz hossain ne kaha ki sena ke itane jawan shahid hue, unke antim sanskaar main to congress netaa or rahul gandhi nahin gaye
 If someone has committed suicide, they are doing politics
 shahanwaaz kaa nishaanaa thodaa sahi jagah laga he
 The comments bhaajapa netaa nalin kohli ne kaha ki ghatana dukhad he magar ye congress ke liye photo oparchunity ban gaya he
 But even after this criticism of Congress BJP, it has started looking active in this matter
 aam aadmi party bhi kaaphi sakriy he
 Returning from Bhiwani, in the evening, Rahul Gandhi has led a candle march at Jantar Mantar
 lekin rahul gandhi ko police ne apni girftar main le liya
 Rahul Gandhi has been detained for the third time in two days
 rahul gandhi ko sansad maarg thane main le jaaya gaya, baad main tughlaq road thane le jaae gaye
 He owns a house on Tughlaq Road
 pravaktaa manish tiwari ne kaha ki yah aghoshit apatkaal he
 Tiwari said that if political people do not express consolation then who else will
 vaise jantar mantar par candal march se pehle hiraasat main lene kaa kya tuk he
 There is a plea that this demonstration was not allowed
 congress kahati he ijazat lee gai thi

 Vikas Verma, candidate for the post of teacher, said, 'we are demanding 75,000 recruitments, but it has been more than 90 days, but no assurance has been received from the government, nor have they fulfilled their promise
 is'
 naukari maangane waalon kii is bheed main siraaj apni roji chalaa lete hai
 They sell water on carts here
 kuch cold drink vagairah bhi bech lete hai
 While living with them, they have also come to know their troubles
 ye khud bhi inaki naukari ke liye duaen karte hai
 Siraj says, "there should be justice with these people
" itane dinon se bhukhe-pyaase barish main pade rahete hai
 But if these people get justice and they will leave from here then how will your work go? In response to this question, Siraj says that 'a lot of people keep bringing their pain and pain here
 takalif ham logon ko bhi hoti he ki bechaare apana ghar chhodkar yahaan aate hai
 So many days are spent
 sarkaar in logon kii jaldi sunwaayee kare
 
 in logon kaa kaam kare
 We will get some other work
 
 will that do'
 nai sarkaar main yoga kii baat aage badi
 
 piem modi khud usamen shaamil hue to bachaler of physical ajukeshan kii degree vaale dedh lakh logon kii ummid jaagi ki unki naukari kii maang badhegi, lekani yahaan to jin 32,000 logon kaa imtihaan hua, unki hi naukari khatai main pad gai
 dpendra Pratap Yadav, Chairman of BPED Sangharsh Morcha, said that 'on the one hand, Honorable Yogi Ji and Hon'ble Prime Minister celebrate Yoga Day on 21 June to promote Yoga
 
 Coming to the ground and sitting on their own
 
 We try to show the public that we promote yoga, but until the appointment of physical teachers, children of poor families studying in school, how can they be taught yoga '
 tippaniyan The new government alleges that during the Akhilesh government, there have been a large number of disturbances in the recruitment
 tamaam bhartiyon par adaalaton ne roak lagaai thi
 The chairman of the UP Public Service Commission was also removed by the court in the charges of recruitment
 aise main in bhartiyon main paardarshita or eemaandaaree kii jaanch kii ja rahi he
 bjp's media in-charge Harishchandra Shrivastava said, 'the kind of corruption that was involved in appointments in the Samajwadi Party government was common
 yogya bachche kunthit ho rahe the
 The agenda of Yogi ji's government is very clear that we should provide a transparent system
 us paardarshee vyavastha main taaki nishpaksh niyuktiyaan ho saken
 Those who are qualified candidates can get a place '
 bipied sangharsh morcha ke adhyaksh dhirendra pratap yadav kehete hai ki 'hamaare liye 32,000 pad srujit kar shasnadesh tak jari ho gaya
 We filled the form and as soon as the power change happened, the government of Honorable Yogi was formed and from then this recruitment process was stopped
 dariyaa kinare lage tambu barish ke pani se gir chuke hai
 All the tents are uprooted
 
 Some are engaged in drying their soaked tents, while others have sheltered under a nearby flyover
 pichhali hukumat main bhi inhen naukari maangane par laathiyaan milti thim
 There are sticks in this government too
 adhinsth seva chayan ayog ne kareeb 11,500 naukariyaan nikaalin
 About 4,000 people passed the written examination, some were interviewed, but recruitment was stopped
 junior assistant pad ke ummidavaar suraj pandey kaa kahana he ki 'ham sabhi vidhyaarthiyon kaa bhavishya adhar main duba hua he
 Do not understand whether the government wants to give us jobs or not
 ham log isi aashwaasan par abhi bhi tike hue hai ki sarkaar hamen ek acchhee si naukari uplabdh karaayegi, lekin samaysima bahut lambii khinchati ja rahi he
 Will we the lives of the unemployed go on like this? vahiin, junior assistant pad ke ummidavaar amit yadav ne kaha ki 'hamaare parivaar main sab ummid laga kar baithe hai
 People are eagerly sitting in everyone's homes
 ham berozegaar chaatr hai
 If one of us does not come forward, how will we take our demands to the government? dariyaa kinare sannaate main lage apane khemon main ye chaatr rahete hai
 From here their voice reaches the government only through the media

 In the new government, the matter of yoga went ahead
 
 When PM Modi himself joined it, one and a half lakh people with a Bachelor of Physical Education degree would be hoping that the demand for their jobs would increase, but only 32,000 people who were tested here got their job lost
 bipied sangharsh morcha ke adhyaksh dhirendra pratap yadav kaa kahana he ki 'ek taraf to mananeey yogi ji or mananeey pradhanmantri ji yoga ko badhaava dene ke liye 21 june ko yoga diwas manaate hai
 
 jameen par aakar khud baithte hai
 
 janata ko ye dikhaane kaa prayaas karte hai ki ham yoga ko badhaava dete hai, lekin jab tak shaareerik shikshakon kii niyukti nahin hogi, jo garib pariwaron ke bachche skool main pard rahe hai, unako yoga kaise sikhaaya ja saktaa he'
 The comments nai sarkaar kaa iljaam he ki akhilesh sarkaar ke dauraan bhartiyon main bahut bade paimaane par gadbadiyaan hui hai
 All the recruitments were banned by the courts
 upi public sarvice kamishan ke chairman ko bhi bhartiyon main ghotaale ke iljaam main adaalat ne hataaya
 In such a situation, transparency and honesty is being investigated in these recruitments
 bhaajapa ke media incharge harishchandra shrivastav ne kaha ki, 'jis tarah kaa bhrashtachar samaajawaadee party kii sarkaar main niyuktiyon ko lekar tha, vah aam tha
 Eligible children were getting frustrated
 yogi ji kii sarkaar kaa agenda bilkul saaf he ki ham ek paardarshee vyavastha den
 In that transparent arrangement so that fair appointments can be made
 jo yogya abhyarthi hai, unako sthaan mil sake'

 - vaivaahik jivan aurprem sambandhonko acha banane ke liye ise manaaya jaataa he
 - Phulera Duj is also considered to be the Abuja Muhurta of the year, any auspicious work can be done on this day

 2 percent
 ye de shift karne waalon ke 7
 Much higher than 6 percent
 vahiin berozegaar logon kaa glismik count 7
 5 percent has been measured
